       if (typeof jQuery != 'undefined') {
 
    console.log("jQuery library is loaded!");

//$(document).ready(function(){

	jQuery(".bottom-arrow").mouseenter(function(){
		var $listEle = jQuery(this).parent();
		var activeIdx = $listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li.active").index();
		activeIdx = parseInt(activeIdx)+1;
		var listLen = $listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li").length;
		console.log(activeIdx+" - "+listLen);
		
		if(activeIdx == listLen) {
			/*$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li.active").addClass('hide').removeClass('active');
							
			$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li:nth-child(1)").removeClass('hide').addClass('active');*/
			jQuery(this).addClass('hide');
		} else {
			if(activeIdx == (listLen-1))
				jQuery(this).addClass('hide');
			
			jQuery("li.collapsable.active").find('.top-arrow').removeClass('hide');			
			var tmpIdx = (parseInt(activeIdx)+1);
			$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li.active").addClass('hide').removeClass('active');			
			$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li:nth-child("+tmpIdx+")").removeClass('hide').addClass('active');
		}
	});

	jQuery(".top-arrow").mouseenter(function(){	
		var $listEle = jQuery(this).parent();
		var activeIdx = $listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li.active").index();
		activeIdx = parseInt(activeIdx)+1;
		console.log(activeIdx);		
		if(activeIdx == 1) {
			/*$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li.active").addClass('hide').removeClass('active');			
			$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li:last-child").removeClass('hide').addClass('active');*/
			jQuery(this).addClass('hide');
		} else {
			if(activeIdx == 2) {
				jQuery(this).addClass('hide');
			}
			
			jQuery("li.collapsable.active").find('.bottom-arrow').removeClass('hide');		
			var tmpIdx = (parseInt(activeIdx)-1);
			
			$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li.active").addClass('hide').removeClass('active');			
			$listEle.find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li:nth-child("+tmpIdx+")").removeClass('hide').addClass('active');
		}
	});
	
	
	jQuery("li.non-collapsable").mouseenter(function(){
		jQuery(this).parent().find(" &gt; li").removeClass('active');
		jQuery(this).addClass('active');
	}).mouseleave(function(){
		jQuery(this).removeClass('active');
	});
		
	jQuery("li.collapsable").mouseenter(function(){
		
		var activeIndx = parseInt(jQuery(this).find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li.active").index()) + 1;
		var listLen = jQuery(this).find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li").length;
		console.log(" ### " + activeIndx + " ### " + jQuery(this).find("ul.section_menus_list &gt; li").length );
		if( listLen == 1) {
			jQuery(this).find('.bottom-arrow').addClass('hide');
			jQuery(this).find('.top-arrow').addClass('hide');
		} else if( activeIndx == listLen ) {
			jQuery(this).find('.bottom-arrow').addClass('hide');
			jQuery(this).find('.top-arrow').removeClass('hide');
		} else if( activeIndx != listLen &amp;&amp; activeIndx &gt; 1 ) {
			jQuery(this).find('.top-arrow').removeClass('hide');
			jQuery(this).find('.bottom-arrow').removeClass('hide');
		} else {
			jQuery(this).find('.top-arrow').addClass('hide');
		}
		
		jQuery("li.collapsable.active").find('div.submenu-content').hide();
		jQuery("li.collapsable.active").removeClass('active');
		
		var tid = jQuery(this).attr('data-tags');
		
		jQuery(this).addClass('active');
		$ele = jQuery(this);
		$ele.find('div.submenu-content').show();
		console.log(" -- "+tid);

	}).mouseleave(function(){
		jQuery(this).removeClass('active');
		jQuery(this).find('div.submenu-content').hide();
	});
 
}else{
 
    console.log("jQuery library is not found!");
 
}

     <h1 class="page-title">
      <a>
       50 of the Best Inspirational and Motivational Quotes
      </a>
     </h1>
     <span>
      Posted by
      <span class="authorship-link">
       <a href="https://www.businessvibes.com/about-businessvibes/authors/nick-huang" target="_blank">
        Nick Huang
       </a>

     <div class="post-content-wrapper " style="width:670px">
      <div class="region region-content">
       <div class="block block-system" id="block-system-main">
        <div class="content">
         <div about="/blog/50-best-inspirational-and-motivational-quotes" class="node node-blog-entry node-promoted" id="node-5347869" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document">
          <span class="rdf-meta element-hidden" content="50 of the Best Inspirational and Motivational Quotes" property="dc:title">
          </span>
          <span class="rdf-meta element-hidden" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" property="sioc:num_replies">
          </span>
          <div class="content clearfix">
           <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden">
            <div class="field-items">
             <div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded">
              <p>
               <a href="https://www.businessvibes.com/blog/best-business-deal-all-time-aba-gets-best-nba" target="_blank">
                <img alt="john-wooden-quotes" src="https://d3bfeozsee0mkq.cloudfront.net/sites/default/files/Wooden.jpeg" style="width: 675px; height: 291px;"/>
               </a>
              </p>
              <p>
               I never took a day off in my twenties. Not one. -
               <em>
                Bill Gates
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               If you see a bandwagon, its too late.
               <em>
                 James Goldsmith
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Even if you are on the right track, youll get run over if you just sit there.
               <em>
                 Will Rogers
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               A man should never neglect his family for business.
               <em>
                 Walt Disney
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Successful people are the ones who are breaking the rules.
               <em>
                 Seth Godin
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Business in a combination of War and sport.
               <em>
                 Andre Maurois
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Hire character. Train skill.
               <em>
                 Peter Schutz
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Your income is directly related to your philosophy, NOT the economy.
               <em>
                 Jim Rohn
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               It is not the strongest of the species that survive, nor the most intelligent,
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               but the one most responsive to change.
               <em>
                 Charles Darwin
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Opportunity is missed by most people because it is dressed in overalls and looks like work.
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               <em>
                 Thomas Edison
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               If you would like to know the value of money, try to borrow some.
               <em>
                 Benjamin Franklin
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Dont worry about failure; you only have to be right once. 
               <em>
                Drew Houston
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Dont play games that you dont understand, even if you see lots of other people making money from them. 
               <em>
                Tony Hsieh
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "The only thing worse than starting something and failing is not starting something. 
               <em>
                Seth Godin
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               The secret to successful hiring is this: look for the people who want to change the world." 
               <em>
                Marc Benioff
               </em>
              </p>
              <p>
               <em>
                <a href="https://www.businessvibes.com/blog/save-money-show-your-employees-you-appreciate-them" target="_blank">
                 <img alt="robert-bosch-quote" src="https://d3bfeozsee0mkq.cloudfront.net/sites/default/files/robert-bosch-quote.jpg" style="width: 675px; height: 288px;"/>
                </a>
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               If you are not embarrassed by the first version of your product, youve launched too late. 
               <em>
                Reid Hoffman
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               As long as youre going to be thinking anyway, think big. 
               <em>
                Donald Trump
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               "There is only one boss. The customer. And he can fire everybody in the company from the chairman on down, simply by spending his money somewhere else." --
               <em>
                Sam Walton
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               Practice does not make perfect. Perfect practice makes perfect. --
               <em>
                Vince Lombardi
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               If you spend your life trying to be good at everything, you will never be great at anything. --
               <em>
                Tom Rath
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               The best way to engage honestly with the marketplace via Twitter is to never use the words "engage," "honestly," or "marketplace. 
               <em>
                Jeffrey Zeldman
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               Early to bed, early to rise, work like hell, and advertise
               <em>
                Ted Turner
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               Don't set your goals by what other people deem important.
               <em>
                Jaachynma N.E. Agu
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               If we only have great companies, we will merely have a prosperous society, not a great one. Economic growth and power are the means, not the definition, of a great nation. --
               <em>
                Jim Collins
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               Create with the heart; build with the mind.
               <em>
                Criss Jami
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               If two men on the same job agree all the time, then one is useless. If they disagree all the time, both are useless.
               <em>
                Darryl F. Zanuck
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               My model for business is The Beatles. They were four guys who kept each other kind of negative tendencies in check. They balanced each other and the total was greater than the sum of the parts. That's how I see business: great things in business are never done by one person, they're done by a team of people.
               <em>
                Steve Jobs
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               Read an hour every day in your chosen field. This works out to about one book per week, fifty books per year, and will guarantee your success.
               <em>
                Brian Tracy
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               A sense of entitlement is a cancerous thought process that is void of gratitude and can be deadly to relationships, businesses, and even nations.
               <em>
                Steve Maraboli
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
               If you first take a minute, an hour or a month to let go of feeling annoyed, frustrated or critical of the person or situation that may be driving you crazy, you set yourself up for much greater leadership and personal success.
               <em>
                John Kuypers
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left:36pt;">
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
               <a href="https://www.businessvibes.com/blog/10-companies-doing-it-right" target="_blank">
                <img alt="bill-gates-quote" src="https://d3bfeozsee0mkq.cloudfront.net/sites/default/files/bill%20gates%20quote_0.jpg" style="width: 675px; height: 287px;"/>
               </a>
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               The man who does not work for the love of work but only for money is not likely to neither make money nor find much fun in life. 
               <em>
                Charles M. Schwab
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Long-range planning works best in the short term. 
               <em>
                Doug Evelyn
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Yesterdays home runs dont win todays games. 
               <em>
                Babe Ruth
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               The golden rule for every business man is this: Put yourself in your customers place. 
               <em>
                Orison Swett Marden
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Leadership is a potent combination of strategy and character. But if you must be without one, be without the strategy. 
               <em>
                Norman Schwarzkopf
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               The person who minds nobodys business but his own is probably a millionaire. -
               <em>
                Anonymous
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               You cannot afford to make the mistake of thinking you cannot be replaced. And your employer cannot afford to have a man around that he cannot afford to do without. 
               <em>
                Frank Irving Fletcher
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               If you think you can, you can. And if you think you cant, youre right. 
               <em>
                Mary Kay Ash
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Somebody once said that in looking for people to hire, you look for three qualities: integrity, intelligence, and energy. And if you dont have the first, the other two will kill you." 
               <em>
                Warren Buffet
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               You have brains in your head, you have feet in your shoes. You can steer yourself in any direction you choose. 
               <em>
                Dr. Seuss
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               Dont tell me the skys the limit when there are footprints on the moon 
               <em>
                Anonymous
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "Dont ask what the world needs. Ask what makes you come alive and go do it. Because what the world needs is more people who have come alive." 
               <em>
                Howard Thurman
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "Ninety-nine percent of failures come from people who have the habit of making excuses." 
               <em>
                George W. Carver
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "It always seems impossible until its done." 
               <em>
                Nelson Mandela
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "At one point in your life you either have the thing you want or the reasons why you dont." 
               <em>
                Andy Roddick
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "There are two kinds of people, those who do the work and those who take the credit. Try to be in the first group; there is less competition there." -
               <em>
                Indira Gandhi
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "You hear about how many fourth quarter comebacks that a guy has and I think it means a guy screwed up in the first three quarters." -
               <em>
                Peyton Manning
               </em>
              </p>
              <p style="margin-left: 36pt;">
               "Nobody is defeated until he starts blaming somebody else. My advice to you is dont fix the blame. Fix the problem.-
               <em>
                John Wooden
               </em>
              </p>
              <p class="rtecenter">
               <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/H5OYqgaJR10?rel=0" width="640">
               </iframe>
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
               <strong>
                You may also like to read:
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
               <a href="https://www.businessvibes.com/blog/5-most-respected-ceo-role-models">
                5 of the Most Respected CEO Role Models
               </a>
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
               <a href="https://www.businessvibes.com/blog/what-generation-y-ceo-might-look">
                What Generation Y CEO Might Look Like
               </a>
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">
               <a href="https://www.businessvibes.com/blog/best-business-deal-all-time-aba-gets-best-nba">
                The Best Business Deal of All-Time?
               </a>
              </p>
              <p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0.0001pt; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">

              </p>

                <a href="http://businessvibes.com/blog">
                 blog for BusinessVibes
                </a>
                . He is a trained writer who graduated University with a degree in media studies and a diploma in journalism.

          var countryCodeGl = "US";
	var countryNameGl = "United States";
	var ptDomn = "https://www.businessvibes.com";
	var ptDomnJs = "https://d3senmqdqm92wb.cloudfront.net";

	jQuery(function(){
		jQuery.ajax( {
			url : "https://www.businessvibes.com/ipinfo",
			type : "GET",
			dataType : 'json',
			cache : false,
			success : function(data) {
				countryCodeGl = "US";
				countryNameGl = "United States of America (USA)";
				
				countryCodeGl = (data._source.country_iso_code != "XX") ? data._source.country_iso_code : "US";
				countryNameGl = (data._source.country_iso_code != "XX") ? data._source.country_name : "United States of America (USA)";
				
				console.log("API returned : "+data._source.country_iso_code+" Assigning Country Code as "+ countryCodeGl + " -:- "+countryNameGl);

				getJsonData("https://www.businessvibes.com/gpn/services/publicEventsUpcoming.json/4/"+countryCodeGl, 1);
				setTimeout(function(){
					countryNameGl = (countryCodeGl == "XX") ? "United States of America (USA)" : countryNameGl;
					getJsonData("https://www.businessvibes.com/browseportal/O/all/all/"+countryNameGl.replace(/ /g,"-")+"/5@0", 2);
				}, 300);

			},
			error : function(xmlHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
				console.log("ERROR : Request Timeout");
			}
		});
				
	});
	function validateData(item)
	{
		if(item!=undefined  &amp;&amp; item!=null)
		{
			console.log(item);
			if(item.trim()!="undefined" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="Not Specified" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="Any" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="-" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="0000-00-00" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="Not Found" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="N/A" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="n/a" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="null" &amp;&amp; item.trim()!="0"){
				return true;
			} else {
				return false;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			return false;
		}
	}

	function getJsonData(url, flag) {
		console.log("URL : "+url);
		jQuery.ajax( {
			url : url,
			type : "GET",
			dataType : 'json',
			cache : false,
			success : function(data) {
				console.log("json succes");
				if(flag == 1) 
					getEventsList(data);
				if(flag == 2)
					getCompaniesList(data);
			}
	    });
	}

	function getEventsList(data) {
		console.log("@getEventsList");
		console.log(data);
		
		var count = 0;
		var content = "";
		var temp = "";

		try {
			
			console.log("@ TRY");
			
			jQuery.each(data['WTradeEvent'],function(i, item) {
				console.log("INSIDE LOOP "+i);
				var tradecomplete = item.urlName;
				var tradeEvevntName = item.tradeEvevntName;
					tradeEvevntName = (tradeEvevntName.length &gt; 25) ? tradeEvevntName.substring(0, 26) + '...' : tradeEvevntName;

				var urlName = ptDomn+"/eventprofile/"+ tradecomplete; //item.urlName;
				var eventLogoParams = item.eventLogoParams;
				var startDate = item.startDate;					
				var logoname = "";
				var venue="";
				var eventTypeName="";
				var eventDescription="";
				var eventTypeName="";
				var industryId="";
				
				if(validateData(item.venue)) {
					venue = item.venue;
					venue = (venue.length &gt; 30) ? venue.substring(0, 27) + '...' : venue;
					venue = "&lt;span&gt;&lt;b&gt;Venue&lt;/b&gt;: "+venue+"&lt;/span&gt;";
				}	
					
				if(validateData(item.eventTypeName)) {
						eventTypeName="&lt;span&gt;EventType: "+item.eventTypeName+"&lt;/span&gt;";
				}					
					/*
				if(validateData(item.eventDescription)) {
					eventDescription="&lt;span&gt;"+item.eventDescription.substring(0, 300).replace(/&lt;\/?[^&gt;]+(&gt;|$)/g, "")+"&lt;/span&gt;";
				}
				if(eventDescription != "") {
					eventDescription = "&lt;div class=\"clearfix group\"&gt;"+eventDescription+"&lt;/div&gt;";
				}
				*/
				var newStartDate = "";
				if(startDate != undefined &amp;&amp; startDate != "" &amp;&amp; startDate != "0000-00-00"){
					startDate = startDate.split(" ");
					newStartDate = "&lt;span&gt;&lt;b&gt;Date&lt;/b&gt; :"+startDate[0]+ " " + startDate[1].substring(0, 3)+ " " + startDate[2]+" &lt;/span&gt;";
				}
					
				console.log("venue :"+venue+";newStartDate :"+newStartDate+";eventTypeName :"+eventTypeName);
				
				if (count &lt;= 3) {
					console.log("count &lt; "+count);
					
						if(item.eventLogoName != undefined) {
							
							logoname = item.eventLogoName;
							if (logoname.indexOf("https://www.businessvibes.com") == -1) {
								logoname = "";
							}
							if (logoname == "") 
							{
								console.log("if logo");
								content += "&lt;li class=\"clearfix group\"&gt;"
										+"&lt;div class=\"margin_top_default\" &gt;"
											
											+"&lt;div class=\"image-area\"&gt;"
												+"&lt;a href=\""+urlName+"\"&gt;"
												+"&lt;img src=\"https://d3senmqdqm92wb.cloudfront.net/profileimg/c_default_logo.png\" /&gt;"
												+"&lt;/a&gt;"
											+"&lt;/div&gt;"
											
											+"&lt;div class=\"clearfix group\" style=\"float:left;width:200px;\" &gt;"
												+"&lt;div&gt;&lt;a class=\"title_link\" target=\"_blank\" href=\""+urlName+"\" onclick=\"_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Event-profile', 'UpcomingEvent-'companyprofile, 'b2bdeals']);\" class=\"data_name_new\" &gt;"+tradeEvevntName+"&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;"
												//+eventDescription

											+"&lt;/div&gt;"

        <script type="text/javascript">
         /* ------------------ Registration ------------------- */
// email
function validateRegEmail(){
	var RegExp =/^[a-z0-9_\+-]+(\.[a-z0-9_\+-]+)*@[a-z0-9-]+(\.[a-z0-9-]+)*\.([a-z]{2,4})$/;
	var url = document.getElementById('regemail').value.trim();
	url = url.toLowerCase();

	if(url == "" || url == "Enter your professional email"){
		jQuery("#e_regemail").remove();
		jQuery("#registration").after("&lt;span id='e_regemail' class='ValidationErrors'&gt;Please enter Email ID&lt;/span&gt;");
		jQuery(".join_businessvibes").css("padding-bottom","25px");
		setTimeout(function(){
		  jQuery('span#e_regemail').remove();
		  jQuery(".join_businessvibes").css("padding-bottom","10px");
		}, 10000);
		
	} else if(!RegExp.test(url)){
		jQuery("#e_regemail").remove();
		jQuery("#registration").after("&lt;span id='e_regemail' class='ValidationErrors'&gt;Please enter valid Email Id&lt;/span&gt;");
		jQuery(".join_businessvibes").css("padding-bottom","25px");
		setTimeout(function(){
		  jQuery('span#e_regemail').remove();
		  jQuery(".join_businessvibes").css("padding-bottom","10px");
		}, 10000);
	} else{
		return true;
	}

}

function validate_regfrm(){
		emailValidationResult = validateRegEmail();
		
		if(emailValidationResult == true)
		{
			regemail=jQuery("#regemail").val();
            window.location.href='/registration?emailId='+regemail;
            //exit(0);
			/*
			regemail=jQuery("#regemail").val();
			regaction=jQuery("button#registration").text();
//			$('#registration_loading').removeClass('endloading');
			jQuery("div#loading_bar_rsb").removeClass("hidden"); 
			jQuery.post("/sites/all/themes/businessvibes/files/getData.php",{regemail:regemail,regaction:regaction},function(regresult){
//			    $("span").html(result);
			    if(regresult== -1)
				{
					jQuery("#e_regemail").remove();
					jQuery("div#loading_bar_rsb").addClass("hidden"); 
					jQuery("#registration").after("&lt;span id='e_regemail' class='ValidationErrors'&gt;Already registered. Please login or click on &lt;a href='/forgot-password' style='float: none;' &gt;Forgot your password?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;");
					document.getElementById("regemail").value = "Thank You";
					setTimeout(function(){
					  jQuery('span#e_regemail').remove();
					}, 10000);
				}
			    else if(regresult== 0)
				{
					jQuery("#e_regemail").remove();
					jQuery("div#loading_bar_rsb").addClass("hidden"); 
					jQuery("#registration").after("&lt;span id='e_regemail' class='msgSucces'&gt;Your confirmation link has been sent to "+regemail+". Please check your email and validate the link immediately.&lt;a  onclick=reSendMail(regemail); class='span_link'&gt;Click here to resend&lt;/a&gt;");
					document.getElementById("regemail").value = "Thank You";
					setTimeout(function(){
					  jQuery('span#e_regemail').remove();
					}, 10000);
					
				}
			    else if(regresult== 2)
				{
					jQuery("#e_regemail").remove();
					jQuery("div#loading_bar_rsb").addClass("hidden"); 
					jQuery("#registration").after("&lt;span id='e_regemail' class='ValidationErrors'&gt;Already registered. Please login or click on &lt;a href='/forgot-password' style='float: none;' &gt;Forgot your password?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;");
					document.getElementById("regemail").value = "Thank You";
					setTimeout(function(){
					  jQuery('span#e_regemail').remove();
					}, 10000);
					
				}
			    else if(regresult== 3)
				{
					jQuery("#e_regemail").remove();
					jQuery("div#loading_bar_rsb").addClass("hidden"); 
					jQuery("#registration").after("&lt;span id='e_regemail' class='msgSucces'&gt;Already registered. &lt;a href='' onclick=reSendMail(regemail); &gt;Click here to resend&lt;/a&gt;");
					document.getElementById("regemail").value = "Thank You";
					setTimeout(function(){
					  jQuery('span#e_regemail').remove();
					}, 10000);
					
				}
			    else
				{
					alert("Invalid Output"+regresult);
				}
			  });
            */
		} // End Of if
	
}  // End of function validate_regfrm

// Fire the function on Press Enter button
jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
	jQuery('#regemail').keypress(function(e) {
	    if(e.which == 13) {
	        validate_regfrm();
	    }
	});

	jQuery('input#regemail').focus(function() {
	  jQuery("input#regemail").removeClass('error');
//	  jQuery("input#regemail").removeClass('succes');
	  jQuery("span#e_regemail").remove(); 
	});

});

//Resend confirmation mail
function reSendMail(remail){
	regemail1=remail;
//	regaction='Register';
//	$.post("getData.php",{regemail:regemail,regaction:regaction},function(result){
//	alert(result);
//	}

$.post("/sites/all/themes/businessvibes/files/getData.php",{resendemail:regemail1},function(result){result;})

}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function footerToggle(id, idx) {
	$("div.tabs").css('display','none');
	$("div#"+id).css('display','block');
	$(".cp_nav span").removeClass('cp_name_current_comp_footer');
	$(".cp_name_nav_"+idx+" span").addClass('cp_name_current_comp_footer');
}

function getLatestNews(id){
	
	jQuery.ajax({
		url :ptDomn+"/blogfetch/18",
		type : "GET",
		dataType : 'json',
		crossDomain: true,
		success : function(data) {
			console.log("########################");
			console.log(data);
		try{
			var columnCount = 0, maxColumns = 4, liCount = 0, content="";
			
			$("#"+id).html("");
			console.log("########################");
			var resultCount = data.blog_posts.length;
			jQuery.each(data.blog_posts, function(e, item){
				
				if( liCount &lt; 5 &amp;&amp; columnCount != maxColumns &amp;&amp; item.post_title != undefined 
						&amp;&amp; item.post_title != null &amp;&amp; item.post_title != "null") {
					
					console.log(item.post_title);
					
					if(item.post_title.length &gt; 35){
                        var modifyText = item.post_title.substr(0, 25);
                        modifyText = modifyText.substr( 0,modifyText.lastIndexOf(" ")+1 );
                        content += '&lt;li&gt;&lt;a target="_blank" href="'+ptDomn+'/'+ item.post_url + '"&gt; ' + modifyText + " ...&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;";
                    } else {
                        content += '&lt;li&gt;&lt;a target="_blank" href="'+ptDomn+'/'+ item.post_url + '"&gt; ' + item.post_title + " ...&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;";
                    }
 
					liCount++;
					
					if( liCount == 4 || resultCount == parseInt(e+1) ){
						liCount = 0;
						$("#"+id).append('&lt;div class="footer_links_block"&gt;&lt;ul class="list-style-none"&gt;' + content + '&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
						content = "";
						columnCount++;
					}
				} else {
					console.log("NULLLLLL");
				}
		   });
		}
		catch(e){
			console.log("Latest News"+e);
		}
	}
	
	});	
}
getLatestNews("B2BbyNews");
  </script>
